COMPUTING REVISION NOTES

1. DATA REPRESENTATION
Binary is base-2, using digits 0 and 1.
Denary is base-10.
Hexadecimal is base-16 (0-9, A-F).

Bits and Bytes:
1 bit = 1 binary digit
8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

2. HARDWARE
CPU (Central Processing Unit):
- ALU performs calculations
- CU controls operations
- Registers store temporary data

RAM:
- Volatile memory
- Fast access

ROM:
- Non-volatile
- Stores firmware

Storage:
- HDD uses magnetic platters
- SSD uses flash memory

3. SOFTWARE
System software:
- Operating systems
- Utilities

Application software:
- Word processors
- Web browsers

4. NETWORKING
LAN = Local Area Network
WAN = Wide Area Network

Protocols:
- HTTP/HTTPS (web)
- FTP (file transfer)
- TCP/IP (data communication)

IP Address:
Unique identifier for a device.

5. CYBER SECURITY
Threats:
- Malware
- Phishing
- Brute force attacks

Prevention:
- Firewalls
- Encryption
- Strong passwords

6. PROGRAMMING
Variables store data.
Data types:
- Integer
- Float
- String
- Boolean

Control structures:
- Sequence
- Selection (if statements)
- Iteration (loops)

7. DATABASES
Fields = individual data items
Records = row of fields
Tables store records

Primary key:
Unique identifier

8. ALGORITHMS
Step-by-step instructions to solve a problem.

Search algorithms:
- Linear search
- Binary search

Sorting algorithms:
- Bubble sort
- Merge sort

1 bit = 1 binary digit
8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

- Registers store temporary data

- Fast access

- Non-volatile
- Stores firmware

8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

- Stores firmware

Binary is base-2, using digits 0 and 1.
Denary is base-10.
Hexadecimal is base-16 (0-9, A-F).

Bits and Bytes:
1 bit = 1 binary digit
8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

2. HARDWARE
CPU (Central Processing Unit):
- ALU performs calculations
- CU controls operations
- Registers store temporary data

RAM:
- Volatile memory
- Fast access

ROM:
- Non-volatile
- Stores firmware

Storage:
- HDD uses magnetic platters
- SSD uses flash memory

3. SOFTWARE
System software:
- Operating systems
- Utilities

Application software:
- Word processors
- Web browsers

4. NETWORKING
LAN = Local Area Network
WAN = Wide Area Network

Protocols:
- HTTP/HTTPS (web)
- FTP (file transfer)
- TCP/IP (data communication)

IP Address:
Unique identifier for a device.

5. CYBER SECURITY
Threats:
- Malware
- Phishing
- Brute force attacks

Prevention:
- Firewalls
- Encryption
- Strong passwords

6. PROGRAMMING
Variables store data.
Data types:
- Integer
- Float
- String
- Boolean

Control structures:
- Sequence
- Selection (if statements)
- Iteration (loops)

7. DATABASES
Fields = individual data items
Records = row of fields
Tables store records

Primary key:
Unique identifier

8. ALGORITHMS
Step-by-step instructions to solve a problem.

Search algorithms:
- Linear search
- Binary search

Sorting algorithms:
- Bubble sort
- Merge sort

1 bit = 1 binary digit
8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

- Registers store temporary data

- Fast access

- Non-volatile
- Stores firmware

8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

- Stores firmware

Binary is base-2, using digits 0 and 1.
Denary is base-10.
Hexadecimal is base-16 (0-9, A-F).

Bits and Bytes:
1 bit = 1 binary digit
8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

2. HARDWARE
CPU (Central Processing Unit):
- ALU performs calculations
- CU controls operations
- Registers store temporary data

RAM:
- Volatile memory
- Fast access

ROM:
- Non-volatile
- Stores firmware

Storage:
- HDD uses magnetic platters
- SSD uses flash memory

3. SOFTWARE
System software:
- Operating systems
- Utilities

Application software:
- Word processors
- Web browsers

4. NETWORKING
LAN = Local Area Network
WAN = Wide Area Network

Protocols:
- HTTP/HTTPS (web)
- FTP (file transfer)
- TCP/IP (data communication)

IP Address:
Unique identifier for a device.

5. CYBER SECURITY
Threats:
- Malware
- Phishing
- Brute force attacks

Prevention:
- Firewalls
- Encryption
- Strong passwords

6. PROGRAMMING
Variables store data.
Data types:
- Integer
- Float
- String
- Boolean

Control structures:
- Sequence
- Selection (if statements)
- Iteration (loops)

7. DATABASES
Fields = individual data items
Records = row of fields
Tables store records

Primary key:
Unique identifier

8. ALGORITHMS
Step-by-step instructions to solve a problem.

Search algorithms:
- Linear search
- Binary search

Sorting algorithms:
- Bubble sort
- Merge sort

1 bit = 1 binary digit
8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

- Registers store temporary data

- Fast access

- Non-volatile
- Stores firmware

8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

- Stores firmware

Binary is base-2, using digits 0 and 1.
Denary is base-10.
Hexadecimal is base-16 (0-9, A-F).

Bits and Bytes:
1 bit = 1 binary digit
8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

2. HARDWARE
CPU (Central Processing Unit):
- ALU performs calculations
- CU controls operations
- Registers store temporary data

RAM:
- Volatile memory
- Fast access

ROM:
- Non-volatile
- Stores firmware

Storage:
- HDD uses magnetic platters
- SSD uses flash memory

3. SOFTWARE
System software:
- Operating systems
- Utilities

Application software:
- Word processors
- Web browsers

4. NETWORKING
LAN = Local Area Network
WAN = Wide Area Network

Protocols:
- HTTP/HTTPS (web)
- FTP (file transfer)
- TCP/IP (data communication)

IP Address:
Unique identifier for a device.

5. CYBER SECURITY
Threats:
- Malware
- Phishing
- Brute force attacks

Prevention:
- Firewalls
- Encryption
- Strong passwords

6. PROGRAMMING
Variables store data.
Data types:
- Integer
- Float
- String
- Boolean

Control structures:
- Sequence
- Selection (if statements)
- Iteration (loops)

7. DATABASES
Fields = individual data items
Records = row of fields
Tables store records

Primary key:
Unique identifier

8. ALGORITHMS
Step-by-step instructions to solve a problem.

Search algorithms:
- Linear search
- Binary search

Sorting algorithms:
- Bubble sort
- Merge sort

8. ALGORITHMS
Step-by-step instructions to solve a problem.

Search algorithms:
- Linear search
- Binary search

Sorting algorithms:
- Bubble sort
- Merge sort
COMPUTING REVISION NOTES

1. DATA REPRESENTATION
Binary is base-2, using digits 0 and 1.
Denary is base-10.
Hexadecimal is base-16 (0-9, A-F).

Bits and Bytes:
1 bit = 1 binary digit
8 bits = 1 byte
1024 bytes = 1 KB

2. HARDWARE
CPU (Central Processing Unit):
- ALU performs calculations
- CU controls operations
- Registers store temporary data

RAM:
- Volatile memory
- Fast access

ROM:
- Non-volatile
- Stores firmware

Storage:
- HDD uses magnetic platters
- SSD uses flash memory

3. SOFTWARE
System software:
- Operating systems
- Utilities

Application software:
- Word processors
- Web browsers

4. NETWORKING
LAN = Local Area Network
WAN = Wide Area Network

Protocols:
- HTTP/HTTPS (web)
- FTP (file transfer)
- TCP/IP (data communication)

IP Address:
Unique identifier for a device.

5. CYBER SECURITY
Threats:
- Malware
- Phishing
- Brute force attacks

Prevention:
- Firewalls
- Encryption
- Strong passwords

6. PROGRAMMING
Variables store data.
Data types:
- Integer
- Float
- String
- Boolean

Control structures:
- Sequence
- Selection (if statements)
- Iteration (loops)

7. DATABASES
Fields = individual data items
Records = row of fields
Tables store records

Primary key:
Unique identifier

8. ALGORITHMS
Step-by-step instructions to solve a problem.

Search algorithms:
- Linear search
- Binary search

Sorting algorithms:
- Bubble sort
- Merge sort
